\begin{register}{H}{SOC\_ETM\_CLK\_EN\_REG}{0x0220}\label{regdesc:SOCETMCLKENREG}
\regfield{\rotatebox{20}{(reserved)}}{31}{1}{0000000000000000000000000000000}%
\regfield{\rotatebox{20}{SOC\_ETM\_CLK\_EN}}{1}{0}{{0}}%
\reglabel{Reset}\regnewline%
\begin{regdesc}\begin{reglist}
\label{fielddesc:SOCETMCLKEN}\item [SOC\_ETM\_CLK\_EN] Configures resister clock gating.\\
0: Support clock only when application writes registers\\
1: Force on clock gating for registers\\ (R/W)
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}
